When information is required that uniquely identifies you as an individual (name, address, phone number, etc), \n\nyou will have the opportunity to \"opt-out\" of any promotional marketing, except when you specifically request marketing or promotional information.</p>\n\n<p>From time to time, Schneider Electric will perform statistical analysis using data provided by you for the purposes of: determining interest in various services provided by \n\nSchneider Electric, inform advertisers of the effectiveness of their marketing campaigns, and to better serve your information needs. Also, Schneider Electric may allow select \n\nthird parties to offer subscription services or fee-based products through the Site. Schneider Electric makes no guarantees in regard to the policies of these parties, so you \n\nshould investigate each site's privacy policy before providing personally identifiable information to third parties. Notwithstanding the foregoing, Schneider Electric does not \n\nsell or rent your personal information to third parties.</p>\n\n<p>Schneider Electric may disclose your personal information if required to do so by law or in the good-faith belief that such action is necessary to: (a) conform with the \n\nedicts of law or comply with legal process served on Schneider Electric or the Site; (b) protect or defend the rights of property of Schneider Electric and its web sites; or (c) \n\nact in urgent circumstances to protect the personal safety of Schneider Electric employees, users of Schneider Electric products or services, or members of the general \n\npublic.</p>\n\n<p>At times Schneider Electric may allow customer to subscribe and/or pay for services through the Site. Schneider Electric will retain and use your \n\npersonal information as necessary to comply with its legal obligations, resolve disputes, and enforce its agreements. Cookies are small text files sent from Schneider \n\nElectric to your hard drive. These files do not allow anyone else to obtain your personal information, nor do they cause any harm to your computer. Schneider Electric may \n\nprovide user data obtained using cookies to third parties, but this information will not include your personally identifiable information.</p>\n\n<p>Third parties may use cookies, web beacons, and similar technologies to collect or receive user data from the Site and elsewhere on the internet and use that information to \n\nprovide measurement services and target ads.
